async function _loadAccSvcSection(){
  var el=document.getElementById('accSvcList');
  if(!el)return;
  var serverCreds=[];
  if(FP_USER&&FP_USER.telegram_id){
    try{
      var r=await apiFetch('/api/me/credentials');
      var d2=await r.json();
      serverCreds=d2.credentials||[];
    }catch(e){}
  }
  // Merge: server creds + local ACC_DATA (server wins)
  var merged={};
  // Local first
  for(var ak in ACC_DATA){if(ak.indexOf('svcLogin_')===0){var sPid=ak.replace('svcLogin_','');if(ACC_DATA[ak])merged[sPid]={pid:sPid,login:ACC_DATA[ak],password:ACC_DATA['svcPass_'+sPid]||'',extra_info:'',backup_codes:'',source:'local'};}}
  // Server overwrites (skip ps_account_* — those go to PS section)
  for(var si=0;si<serverCreds.length;si++){
    var sc=serverCreds[si];
    if(sc.product_id.indexOf('ps_account_')===0)continue;
    merged[sc.product_id]={pid:sc.product_id,login:sc.login||'',password:sc.password||'',extra_info:sc.extra_info||'',backup_codes:sc.backup_codes||'',product_name:sc.product_name||'',product_photo:sc.product_photo||'',source:'server'};
    // Auto-save to ACC_DATA
    if(sc.login){ACC_DATA['svcLogin_'+sc.product_id]=sc.login;}
    if(sc.password){ACC_DATA['svcPass_'+sc.product_id]=sc.password;}
    if(sc.backup_codes){ACC_DATA['backupCodes_'+sc.product_id]=sc.backup_codes.split('\n').filter(function(c){return c.trim()});}
    saveAccData();
  }
  var pids=Object.keys(merged);
  if(!pids.length){
    el.innerHTML='<div style="font-size:13px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.6);margin-bottom:14px;line-height:1.5">Аккаунты от нейросетей и сервисов появятся здесь автоматически после покупки</div>'
    +'<div style="border-radius:16px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.06);border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.1);overflow:hidden">'
    +'<div style="padding:24px 20px 20px;display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;gap:12px">'
    +'<div style="display:flex;gap:8px">'
    +'<div style="width:44px;height:44px;border-radius:12px;background:linear-gradient(135deg,rgba(110,86,255,.6),rgba(168,85,247,.4));display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:20px">🎵</div>'
    +'<div style="width:44px;height:44px;border-radius:12px;background:linear-gradient(135deg,rgba(110,86,255,.6),rgba(168,85,247,.4));display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:20px">🎬</div>'
    +'<div style="width:44px;height:44px;border-radius:12px;background:linear-gradient(135deg,rgba(110,86,255,.6),rgba(168,85,247,.4));display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:20px">☁️</div>'
    +'</div>'
    +'<div style="text-align:center">'
    +'<div style="font-size:15px;font-weight:700;color:rgba(255,255,255,.9);margin-bottom:6px">Аккаунты появятся после покупки</div>'
    +'<div style="font-size:13px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.55);line-height:1.5">ChatGPT, Spotify, Netflix и другие сервисы<br>будут храниться здесь в одном месте</div>'
    +'</div>'
    +'</div>'
    +'<div onclick="switchTab(\'catalog\')" style="border-top:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.08);padding:12px 20px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;gap:6px;cursor:pointer">'
    +'<span style="font-size:13px;color:rgba(110,86,255,1);font-weight:600">Перейти в каталог</span>'
    +'<span style="font-size:13px;color:rgba(110,86,255,1)">→</span>'
    +'</div>'
    +'</div>';
    return;
  }
  // Store merged data globally for edit/delete
  window._svcMerged=merged;
  window._svcPids=pids;
  _renderSvcCards(el,merged,pids);
}

function _renderSvcCards(el,merged,pids){
  var h2='<div style="font-size:13px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.6);margin-bottom:14px;line-height:1.5">Аккаунты от сервисов</div>';
  for(var pi=0;pi<pids.length;pi++){
    var m=merged[pids[pi]];
    var spP=D?D.products[m.pid]:null;
    var spName=m.product_name||(spP?spP.name:m.pid);
    var spPhoto=m.product_photo||(spP?(spP.photo||spP.image||''):'');
    var safeId=m.pid.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g,'_');
    var isEditing=!!window['_svcEdit_'+safeId];

    h2+='<div id="svcCard_'+safeId+'" style="border-radius:14px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.04);border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.08);padding:16px;margin-bottom:12px">';
    h2+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;margin-bottom:12px">';
    if(spPhoto)h2+='<img src="'+es(spPhoto)+'" style="width:36px;height:36px;border-radius:10px;object-fit:cover" onerror="this.style.display=\'none\'">';
    h2+='<div style="font-size:14px;font-weight:700;flex:1">'+es(spName)+'</div>';
    h2+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px">';
    if(!isEditing){
      h2+='<button onclick="_svcStartEdit(\''+es(m.pid)+'\')" style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;padding:4px;display:flex;align-items:center" title="Редактировать"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="rgba(255,255,255,.4)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M11 4H4a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v14a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h14a2 2 0 0 0 2-2v-7"/><path d="M18.5 2.5a2.121 2.121 0 0 1 3 3L12 15l-4 1 1-4 9.5-9.5z"/></svg></button>';
    }
    h2+='<button onclick="_svcDeleteCred(\''+es(m.pid)+'\',\''+es(spName)+'\')" style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;padding:4px;display:flex;align-items:center" title="Удалить"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="rgba(255,80,80,.5)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><polyline points="3 6 5 6 21 6"/><path d="M19 6v14a2 2 0 0 1-2 2H7a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V6m3 0V4a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h4a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v2"/><line x1="10" y1="11" x2="10" y2="17"/><line x1="14" y1="11" x2="14" y2="17"/></svg></button>';
    h2+='</div></div>';

    if(isEditing){
      h2+='<div style="margin-bottom:10px"><div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.4);margin-bottom:4px">Логин</div>';
      h2+='<input class="cart-input" id="svcEditLogin_'+safeId+'" value="'+es(m.login||'')+'" placeholder="Логин" style="margin-bottom:0;font-size:13px"></div>';
      h2+='<div style="margin-bottom:10px"><div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.4);margin-bottom:4px">Пароль</div>';
      h2+='<input class="cart-input" id="svcEditPass_'+safeId+'" value="'+es(m.password||'')+'" placeholder="Пароль" style="margin-bottom:0;font-size:13px"></div>';
      if(m.backup_codes){
        h2+='<div style="margin-bottom:10px"><div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.4);margin-bottom:4px">🔐 Резервные коды</div>';
        h2+='<textarea class="cart-input" id="svcEditCodes_'+safeId+'" rows="3" placeholder="Резервные коды (каждый с новой строки)" style="margin-bottom:0;font-size:12px;font-family:monospace;resize:vertical;min-height:60px">'+es(m.backup_codes)+'</textarea></div>';
      }
      h2+='<div style="display:flex;gap:8px">';
      h2+='<button onclick="_svcSaveEdit(\''+es(m.pid)+'\')" style="flex:1;height:40px;border-radius:10px;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#6e56ff,#a855f7);border:none;color:#fff;font-size:13px;font-weight:700;cursor:pointer;font-family:inherit">Сохранить</button>';
      h2+='<button onclick="_svcCancelEdit(\''+es(m.pid)+'\')" style="height:40px;padding:0 16px;border-radius:10px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.06);border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.1);color:rgba(255,255,255,.6);font-size:13px;font-weight:600;cursor:pointer;font-family:inherit">Отмена</button>';
      h2+='</div>';
    } else {
      if(m.login){
        h2+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:6px">';
        h2+='<div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.4)">Логин</div>';
        h2+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px"><span style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;font-family:monospace">'+es(m.login)+'</span>';
        h2+='<button onclick="navigator.clipboard.writeText(\''+m.login.replace(/'/g,"\\'")+'\');showToast(\'Скопировано\')" style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;padding:2px;display:flex;align-items:center">'+_copySvg+'</button></div></div>';
      }
      if(m.password){
        var pwId='svcPw_'+safeId;
        h2+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:6px">';
        h2+='<div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.4)">Пароль</div>';
        h2+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px"><span id="'+pwId+'" style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;font-family:monospace">••••••</span>';
        h2+='<button onclick="_toggleCredVis(\''+pwId+'\',\''+m.password.replace(/'/g,"\\'")+'\',this)" style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;padding:2px;display:flex;align-items:center">'+_eyeOffSm+'</button>';
        h2+='<button onclick="navigator.clipboard.writeText(\''+m.password.replace(/'/g,"\\'")+'\');showToast(\'Скопировано\')" style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;padding:2px;display:flex;align-items:center">'+_copySvg+'</button></div></div>';
      }
      if(m.extra_info){
        h2+='<div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.4);margin-top:4px">'+m.extra_info.replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/\n/g,'<br>')+'</div>';
      }
      if(m.backup_codes){
        var codes=m.backup_codes.split('\n').filter(function(c){return c.trim()});
        if(codes.length){
          h2+='<div style="margin-top:8px"><div style="font-size:10px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.3);margin-bottom:3px">🔐 Резервные коды</div>';
          h2+='<div style="background:rgba(0,0,0,.2);border-radius:6px;padding:6px 8px;font-family:monospace;font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.6);line-height:1.5">';
          for(var ci2=0;ci2<codes.length;ci2++){h2+=codes[ci2].replace(/</g,'&lt;')+'<br>';}
          h2+='</div>';
          h2+='<button onclick="navigator.clipboard.writeText(\''+m.backup_codes.replace(/'/g,"\\'").replace(/\n/g,'\\n')+'\');showToast(\'Коды скопированы\')" style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;padding:2px 0;margin-top:3px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.35);font-size:11px">'+_copySvg+' Копировать все коды</button>';
          h2+='</div>';
        }
      }
    }
    h2+='</div>';
  }
  el.innerHTML=h2;
}

function _svcStartEdit(pid){
  var safeId=pid.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g,'_');
  window['_svcEdit_'+safeId]=true;
  var el=document.getElementById('accSvcList');
  if(el&&window._svcMerged&&window._svcPids)_renderSvcCards(el,window._svcMerged,window._svcPids);
}
function _svcCancelEdit(pid){
  var safeId=pid.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g,'_');
  delete window['_svcEdit_'+safeId];
  var el=document.getElementById('accSvcList');
  if(el&&window._svcMerged&&window._svcPids)_renderSvcCards(el,window._svcMerged,window._svcPids);
}
async function _svcSaveEdit(pid){
  var safeId=pid.replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g,'_');
  var loginEl=document.getElementById('svcEditLogin_'+safeId);
  var passEl=document.getElementById('svcEditPass_'+safeId);
  var codesEl=document.getElementById('svcEditCodes_'+safeId);
  var newLogin=loginEl?loginEl.value.trim():'';
  var newPass=passEl?passEl.value.trim():'';
  var newCodes=codesEl?codesEl.value.trim():'';
  if(newLogin){ACC_DATA['svcLogin_'+pid]=newLogin;}else{delete ACC_DATA['svcLogin_'+pid];}
  if(newPass){ACC_DATA['svcPass_'+pid]=newPass;}else{delete ACC_DATA['svcPass_'+pid];}
  if(newCodes){ACC_DATA['backupCodes_'+pid]=newCodes.split('\n').filter(function(c){return c.trim()});}else{delete ACC_DATA['backupCodes_'+pid];}
  saveAccData();
  if(FP_USER&&FP_USER.telegram_id){
    try{
      await apiFetch('/api/me/credentials/'+encodeURIComponent(pid),{method:'PUT',body:JSON.stringify({login:newLogin,password:newPass,backup_codes:newCodes})});
    }catch(e){console.error('Save cred error:',e);}
  }
  if(window._svcMerged&&window._svcMerged[pid]){
    window._svcMerged[pid].login=newLogin;
    window._svcMerged[pid].password=newPass;
    window._svcMerged[pid].backup_codes=newCodes;
  }
  delete window['_svcEdit_'+safeId];
  var el=document.getElementById('accSvcList');
  if(el&&window._svcMerged&&window._svcPids)_renderSvcCards(el,window._svcMerged,window._svcPids);
  showToast('Сохранено');
}
function _svcDeleteCred(pid,name){
  if(!confirm('Удалить аккаунт '+(name||pid)+'?'))return;
  delete ACC_DATA['svcLogin_'+pid];
  delete ACC_DATA['svcPass_'+pid];
  delete ACC_DATA['backupCodes_'+pid];
  saveAccData();
  if(FP_USER&&FP_USER.telegram_id){
    apiFetch('/api/me/credentials/'+encodeURIComponent(pid),{method:'DELETE'}).catch(function(){});
  }
  if(window._svcMerged){delete window._svcMerged[pid];}
  if(window._svcPids){window._svcPids=window._svcPids.filter(function(p){return p!==pid});}
  var el=document.getElementById('accSvcList');
  if(el&&window._svcPids&&window._svcPids.length){
    _renderSvcCards(el,window._svcMerged,window._svcPids);
  }else if(el){
    _loadAccSvcSection();
  }
  showToast('Удалено');
}

var _eyeOn='<svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="rgba(255,255,255,.35)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M1 12s4-8 11-8 11 8 11 8-4 8-11 8-11-8-11-8z"/><circle cx="12" cy="12" r="3"/></svg>';
var _eyeOff='<svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="rgba(255,255,255,.2)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M17.94 17.94A10.07 10.07 0 0 1 12 20c-7 0-11-8-11-8a18.45 18.45 0 0 1 5.06-5.94M9.9 4.24A9.12 9.12 0 0 1 12 4c7 0 11 8 11 8a18.5 18.5 0 0 1-2.16 3.19m-6.72-1.07a3 3 0 1 1-4.24-4.24"/><line x1="1" y1="1" x2="23" y2="23"/></svg>';
var _eyeOnSm=_eyeOn.replace(/18/g,'16');
var _eyeOffSm=_eyeOff.replace(/18/g,'16');
var _copySvg='<svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="rgba(255,255,255,.35)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><rect x="9" y="9" width="13" height="13" rx="2" ry="2"/><path d="M5 15H4a2 2 0 0 1-2-2V4a2 2 0 0 1 2-2h9a2 2 0 0 1 2 2v1"/></svg>';
function _togglePassVis(btn){
  var inp=btn.parentElement.querySelector('input');
  if(!inp)return;
  if(inp.type==='password'){inp.type='text';btn.innerHTML=_eyeOn;}
  else{inp.type='password';btn.innerHTML=_eyeOff;}
}
function _toggleCredVis(spanId,realPw,btn){
  var s=document.getElementById(spanId);if(!s)return;
  if(s.textContent==='••••••'){s.textContent=realPw;btn.innerHTML=_eyeOnSm;}
  else{s.textContent='••••••';btn.innerHTML=_eyeOffSm;}
}
function _saveAccFields(){
  var r=(ACC_DATA.psRegion||'TR').toLowerCase();
  var l=document.getElementById('accPsLogin');if(l)ACC_DATA['psLogin_'+r]=l.value;
  var p=document.getElementById('accPsPass');if(p)ACC_DATA['psPass_'+r]=p.value;
  saveAccData(['ps_account_'+r]);
}
function _saveAccSvcFields(){
  var els=document.querySelectorAll('.acc-svc-login');
  for(var i=0;i<els.length;i++){
    var pid=els[i].getAttribute('data-pid');
    ACC_DATA['svcLogin_'+pid]=els[i].value;
    var passEl=document.querySelector('.acc-svc-pass[data-pid="'+pid+'"]');
    if(passEl)ACC_DATA['svcPass_'+pid]=passEl.value;
  }
  saveAccData();
}
function setAccRegion(r){_saveAccFields();ACC_DATA.psRegion=r;saveAccData(['ps_account_'+r.toLowerCase()]);showAccountsPage(true)}
function setAccConsole(c){_saveAccFields();ACC_DATA.psConsole=c;var _cr=(ACC_DATA.psRegion||'TR').toLowerCase();saveAccData(['ps_account_'+_cr]);showAccountsPage(true)}
function saveAccounts(){
  var r=(ACC_DATA.psRegion||'TR').toLowerCase();
  ACC_DATA['psLogin_'+r]=(document.getElementById('accPsLogin')||{}).value||'';
  ACC_DATA['psPass_'+r]=(document.getElementById('accPsPass')||{}).value||'';
  saveAccData(['ps_account_'+r]);
  showToast('Данные сохранены');
}
function addBackupCode(){
  var inp=document.getElementById('newBackupCode');if(!inp||!inp.value.trim())return;
  var r=(ACC_DATA.psRegion||'TR').toLowerCase();
  var key='backupCodes_'+r;
  if(!ACC_DATA[key])ACC_DATA[key]=[];
  ACC_DATA[key].push({code:inp.value.trim(),used:false});
  _saveAccFields();saveAccData(['ps_account_'+r]);var sy=document.getElementById('profilePage').scrollTop;showAccountsPage(true);document.getElementById('profilePage').scrollTop=sy;showToast('Код добавлен');
}
function markCodeUsed(idx){
  var r=(ACC_DATA.psRegion||'TR').toLowerCase();
  var key='backupCodes_'+r;
  if(!ACC_DATA[key]||!ACC_DATA[key][idx])return;
  ACC_DATA[key][idx].used=true;
  _saveAccFields();saveAccData(['ps_account_'+r]);var sy=document.getElementById('profilePage').scrollTop;showAccountsPage(true);document.getElementById('profilePage').scrollTop=sy;
}
function removeCode(idx){
  var r=(ACC_DATA.psRegion||'TR').toLowerCase();
  var key='backupCodes_'+r;
  if(!ACC_DATA[key])return;
  ACC_DATA[key].splice(idx,1);
  _saveAccFields();saveAccData(['ps_account_'+r]);var sy=document.getElementById('profilePage').scrollTop;showAccountsPage(true);document.getElementById('profilePage').scrollTop=sy;showToast('Код удалён');
}
function openHelpLink(type){
  var urls={
    '2fa_setup':'https://telegra.ph/Kak-vklyuchit-dvuhfaktornuyu-autentifikaciyu-akkaunta-PlayStation-04-08',
    'find_codes':'https://telegra.ph/Gde-najti-rezervnye-kody-PlayStation-04-08',
    'update_codes':'https://telegra.ph/Kak-obnovit-rezervnye-kody-PlayStation-04-08'
  };
  var url=urls[type];
  if(url){
    if(window.Telegram&&Telegram.WebApp&&Telegram.WebApp.openLink){Telegram.WebApp.openLink(url,{try_instant_view:true})}
    else{window.open(url,'_blank')}
  } else {showToast('Скоро — статья в разработке')}
}

async function showCashbackHistory(){
  if(!FP_USER||!FP_USER.telegram_id){showToast('Данные загружаются...');return;}
  _profileScrollY=document.getElementById('profilePage').scrollTop;
  document.getElementById('profilePage').scrollTo(0,0);
  tgBack(true,function(){_backToProfile()});
  var h='<div style="padding:20px">';
  h+='<div style="font-size:28px;font-weight:900;letter-spacing:-.3px;margin-bottom:20px">История кэшбэка</div>';

  // Balance card
  h+='<div style="padding:16px;border-radius:14px;background:linear-gradient(135deg,rgba(110,86,255,.12),rgba(168,85,247,.08));border:1px solid rgba(110,86,255,.2);margin-bottom:20px">';
  h+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between">';
  h+='<div><div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.5);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:1px">Текущий баланс</div><div style="font-size:28px;font-weight:800;margin-top:4px">'+FP_USER.balance+' ₽</div></div>';
  h+='<div style="text-align:right"><div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.5)">Всего начислено</div><div style="font-size:18px;font-weight:700;margin-top:4px;color:#a78bfa">'+FP_USER.cashback_total+' ₽</div></div>';
  h+='</div></div>';

  h+='<div id="cashbackHistoryList"><div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.3)">Загрузка...</div></div>';
  h+='<div style="height:80px"></div></div>';
  document.getElementById('profilePage').innerHTML=h;

  // Fetch history
  try {
    var r=await apiFetch('/api/me/cashback-history');
    var d=await r.json();
    var list=d.history||[];
    var el=document.getElementById('cashbackHistoryList');
    if(!el)return;

    if(!list.length){
      el.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px"><div style="font-size:40px;margin-bottom:12px">📭</div><div style="font-size:15px;font-weight:600;color:rgba(255,255,255,.5)">История пуста</div><div style="font-size:12px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.3);margin-top:6px">Начисления появятся после покупок</div></div>';
      return;
    }

    var html='';
    var types={
      purchase:{icon:'🛒',label:'Покупка',color:'#22c55e'},
      referral:{icon:'👤',label:'От друга',color:'#a78bfa'},
      manual:{icon:'💎',label:'Бонус',color:'#60a5fa'},
      mass:{icon:'🎁',label:'Бонус',color:'#fbbf24'},
      promo:{icon:'🎟',label:'Промо',color:'#f472b6'},
      spend:{icon:'💳',label:'Списание',color:'#ef4444'}
    };

    for(var i=0;i<list.length;i++){
      var item=list[i];
      var t=types[item.type]||{icon:'💰',label:item.type,color:'#888'};
      if(item.type==='manual'&&item.amount<0)t={icon:'💳',label:'Списание',color:'#ef4444'};
      var isPositive=item.amount>=0;
      var fromUser=item.from_username?(' @'+item.from_username):(item.from_first_name?(' '+item.from_first_name):'');

      html+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;padding:14px 0;border-bottom:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.06)">';
      var iconHtml='';
      if(item.type==='referral'&&item.from_photo_url){
        iconHtml='<img src="'+item.from_photo_url+'" style="width:44px;height:44px;border-radius:12px;object-fit:cover;flex-shrink:0" onerror="this.outerHTML=\'<div style=\\\'width:44px;height:44px;border-radius:12px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.06);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:20px;flex-shrink:0\\\'>'+t.icon+'</div>\'">';
      } else {
        iconHtml='<div style="width:48px;height:48px;border-radius:12px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.06);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:20px;flex-shrink:0">'+t.icon+'</div>';
      }
      html+=iconHtml;
      html+='<div style="flex:1;min-width:0">';
      html+='<div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:#fff">'+t.label+(fromUser?fromUser:'')+'</div>';
      if(item.comment)html+='<div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.4);margin-top:2px;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap">'+item.comment.replace(/</g,'&lt;')+'</div>';
      html+='<div style="font-size:10px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.25);margin-top:2px">'+new Date(item.created_at).toLocaleString('ru',{day:'numeric',month:'short',hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'})+'</div>';
      html+='</div>';
      html+='<div style="font-size:15px;font-weight:700;color:'+(isPositive?t.color:'#ef4444')+';white-space:nowrap">'+(isPositive?'+':'')+item.amount+' ₽</div>';
      html+='</div>';
    }
    el.innerHTML=html;
  } catch(e){
    var el=document.getElementById('cashbackHistoryList');
    if(el)el.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.3)">Ошибка загрузки</div>';
  }
}
async function showFriendsList(){
  if(!FP_USER||!FP_USER.telegram_id){showToast('Данные загружаются...');return;}
  _profileScrollY=document.getElementById('profilePage').scrollTop;
  document.getElementById('profilePage').scrollTo(0,0);
  tgBack(true,function(){_backToProfile()});
  var h='<div style="padding:20px">';
  h+='<div style="font-size:28px;font-weight:900;letter-spacing:-.3px;margin-bottom:20px">Друзья</div>';
  h+='<div id="friendsListContent"><div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.3)">Загрузка...</div></div>';
  h+='<div style="height:80px"></div></div>';
  document.getElementById('profilePage').innerHTML=h;
  try{
    var r=await apiFetch('/api/me/referrals');
    var d=await r.json();
    var refs=d.referrals||[];
    var el=document.getElementById('friendsListContent');
    if(!el)return;
    if(!refs.length){
      el.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px"><div style="font-size:40px;margin-bottom:12px">👥</div><div style="font-size:15px;font-weight:600;color:rgba(255,255,255,.5)">Пока нет друзей</div><div style="font-size:12px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.3);margin-top:6px">Поделитесь реферальной ссылкой</div></div>';
      return;
    }
    var html='';
    for(var i=0;i<refs.length;i++){
      var f=refs[i];
      var name=(f.first_name||'')+(f.last_name?' '+f.last_name:'');
      var letter=(name||'?').charAt(0).toUpperCase();
      var avatar=f.photo_url
        ?'<img src="'+f.photo_url+'" style="width:44px;height:44px;border-radius:50%;object-fit:cover" onerror="this.style.display=\'none\';this.nextElementSibling.style.display=\'flex\'">'+'<div style="display:none;width:44px;height:44px;border-radius:50%;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#6e56ff,#a855f7);align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:18px;font-weight:700;color:#fff;flex-shrink:0">'+letter+'</div>'
        :'<div style="width:44px;height:44px;border-radius:50%;background:linear-gradient(135deg,#6e56ff,#a855f7);display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:18px;font-weight:700;color:#fff;flex-shrink:0">'+letter+'</div>';
      var earned=f.earned||0;
      var date=f.created_at?new Date(f.created_at).toLocaleDateString('ru',{day:'numeric',month:'short',year:'numeric'}):'';
      html+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;padding:12px 0;border-bottom:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.06)">';
      html+=avatar;
      html+='<div style="flex:1;min-width:0">';
      html+='<div style="font-size:14px;font-weight:600;color:#fff">'+es(name||'Пользователь')+'</div>';
      if(f.username)html+='<div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.4)">@'+es(f.username)+'</div>';
      if(date)html+='<div style="font-size:10px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.25);margin-top:2px">с '+date+'</div>';
      html+='</div>';
      if(earned>0)html+='<div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:#a78bfa;white-space:nowrap">+'+earned+' ₽</div>';
      html+='</div>';
    }
    el.innerHTML=html;
  }catch(e){
    var el=document.getElementById('friendsListContent');
    if(el)el.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.3)">Ошибка загрузки</div>';
  }
}
async function showOrderHistory(){
  if(!FP_USER||!FP_USER.telegram_id){showToast('Данные загружаются...');return;}
  _profileScrollY=document.getElementById('profilePage').scrollTop;
  document.getElementById('profilePage').scrollTo(0,0);
  tgBack(true,function(){_backToProfile()});
  var h='<div style="padding:20px">';
  h+='<div style="font-size:28px;font-weight:900;letter-spacing:-.3px;margin-bottom:20px">История покупок</div>';
  h+='<div id="orderHistoryList"><div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.3)">Загрузка...</div></div>';
  h+='<div style="height:80px"></div></div>';
  document.getElementById('profilePage').innerHTML=h;

  try {
    var r=await apiFetch('/api/me/orders');
    var d=await r.json();
    var orders=d.orders||[];
    var el=document.getElementById('orderHistoryList');
    if(!el)return;

    if(!orders.length){
      el.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:40px"><div style="font-size:40px;margin-bottom:12px">🛍</div><div style="font-size:15px;font-weight:600;color:rgba(255,255,255,.5)">Заказов пока нет</div><div style="font-size:12px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.3);margin-top:6px">Здесь будут все ваши покупки</div></div>';
      return;
    }

    var statusMap={
      'new':{label:'Новый',color:'#fbbf24'},
      'pending_payment':{label:'Ожидает оплаты',color:'#f97316'},
      'paid':{label:'Оплачен',color:'#22c55e'},
      'processing':{label:'В работе',color:'#60a5fa'},
      'done':{label:'Выполнен',color:'#22c55e'},
      'cancelled':{label:'Отменён',color:'#ef4444'}
    };

    var html='';
    for(var i=0;i<orders.length;i++){
      var o=orders[i];
      var st=statusMap[o.status]||{label:o.status,color:'#888'};
      var items=o.items||[];
      var firstItem=items[0]||{};
      var itemCount=items.length;
      var photo='';
      if(firstItem.product_id&&D&&D.products[firstItem.product_id]){photo=D.products[firstItem.product_id].photo||'';}

      html+='<div style="padding:14px;border-radius:14px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.04);border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.07);margin-bottom:10px">';

      // Header: order number + status
      html+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:10px">';
      html+='<div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:rgba(255,255,255,.6)">'+o.order_number+'</div>';
      html+='<div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:600;color:'+st.color+';padding:3px 8px;border-radius:6px;background:'+st.color+'15">'+st.label+'</div>';
      html+='</div>';

      // Items
      for(var j=0;j<items.length;j++){
        var it=items[j];
        var itPhoto='';
        if(it.product_id&&D&&D.products[it.product_id]){itPhoto=D.products[it.product_id].photo||'';}
        html+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;'+(j>0?'margin-top:8px;':'')+'">';
        if(itPhoto)html+='<img src="'+itPhoto+'" style="width:60px;height:60px;border-radius:12px;object-fit:cover;flex-shrink:0" onerror="this.style.display=\'none\'">';
        html+='<div style="flex:1;min-width:0"><div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:#fff;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap">'+((it.name||'').replace(/</g,'&lt;'))+'</div>';
        if(it.variant)html+='<div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.4)">'+((it.variant||'').replace(/</g,'&lt;'))+'</div>';
        html+='</div>';
        html+='<div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:rgba(255,255,255,.7);white-space:nowrap">'+fm(it.price)+'</div>';
        html+='</div>';
      }

      // Footer: total + date
      html+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-top:10px;padding-top:10px;border-top:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.06)">';
      html+='<div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.3)">'+new Date(o.created_at).toLocaleString('ru',{day:'numeric',month:'short',year:'numeric',hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'})+'</div>';
      html+='<div style="font-size:15px;font-weight:700">'+fm(o.total)+'</div>';
      html+='</div>';

      // Credentials placeholder
      html+='<div id="orderCreds_'+o.id+'" style="display:none"></div>';

      html+='</div>';
    }
    el.innerHTML=html;

    // Fetch credentials for each order
    for(var ci=0;ci<orders.length;ci++){
      (function(oid){
        var tgU=FP_USER.telegram_id;
        apiFetch('/api/me/orders/'+oid+'/credentials').then(function(r){return r.json()}).then(function(cd){
          var creds=cd.credentials||[];
          if(!creds.length)return;
          var el2=document.getElementById('orderCreds_'+oid);
          if(!el2)return;
          var ch='<div style="margin-top:10px;padding-top:10px;border-top:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.06)">';
          ch+='<div style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;color:rgba(124,92,252,.9);margin-bottom:8px">🔑 Данные для входа</div>';
          for(var k=0;k<creds.length;k++){
            var cr=creds[k];
            var cpid=cr.product_id||'';
            var pName=(D&&D.products[cpid])?D.products[cpid].name:cpid;
            ch+='<div style="background:rgba(255,255,255,.04);border-radius:10px;padding:10px;margin-bottom:6px">';
            if(creds.length>1)ch+='<div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:600;color:rgba(255,255,255,.5);margin-bottom:6px">'+pName+'</div>';
            if(cr.login){
              ch+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:4px">';
              ch+='<div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.4)">Логин</div>';
              ch+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px"><span style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;font-family:monospace">'+cr.login.replace(/</g,'&lt;')+'</span>';
              ch+='<button onclick="navigator.clipboard.writeText(\''+cr.login.replace(/'/g,"\\'")+'\');showToast(\'Скопировано\')" style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;padding:2px;display:flex;align-items:center">'+_copySvg+'</button></div></div>';
            }
            if(cr.password){
              ch+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:4px">';
              ch+='<div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.4)">Пароль</div>';
              ch+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px"><span id="credPw_'+cr.id+'" style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;font-family:monospace">••••••</span>';
              ch+='<button onclick="_toggleCredVis(\'credPw_'+cr.id+'\',\''+cr.password.replace(/'/g,"\\'")+'\',this)" style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;padding:2px;display:flex;align-items:center">'+_eyeOffSm+'</button>';
              ch+='<button onclick="navigator.clipboard.writeText(\''+cr.password.replace(/'/g,"\\'")+'\');showToast(\'Скопировано\')" style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;padding:2px;display:flex;align-items:center">'+_copySvg+'</button></div></div>';
            }
            if(cr.extra_info){
              ch+='<div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.4);margin-top:4px">'+cr.extra_info.replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/\n/g,'<br>')+'</div>';
            }
            if(cr.backup_codes){
              var codes=cr.backup_codes.split('\n').filter(function(c){return c.trim()});
              if(codes.length){
                ch+='<div style="margin-top:6px"><div style="font-size:10px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.3);margin-bottom:3px">🔐 Резервные коды</div>';
                ch+='<div style="background:rgba(0,0,0,.2);border-radius:6px;padding:6px 8px;font-family:monospace;font-size:11px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.6);line-height:1.5">';
                for(var ci2=0;ci2<codes.length;ci2++){ch+=codes[ci2].replace(/</g,'&lt;')+'<br>';}
                ch+='</div>';
                ch+='<button onclick="navigator.clipboard.writeText(\''+cr.backup_codes.replace(/'/g,"\\'").replace(/\n/g,'\\n')+'\');showToast(\'Коды скопированы\')" style="background:none;border:none;cursor:pointer;padding:2px 0;margin-top:3px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:4px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.35);font-size:11px">'+_copySvg+' Копировать все коды</button>';
                ch+='</div>';
              }
            }
            ch+='</div>';
            // Auto-save to ACC_DATA
            if(cr.login)ACC_DATA['svcLogin_'+cpid]=cr.login;
            if(cr.password)ACC_DATA['svcPass_'+cpid]=cr.password;
            if(cr.backup_codes){
              ACC_DATA['backupCodes_'+cpid]=cr.backup_codes.split('\n').filter(function(c){return c.trim()});
            }
          }
          ch+='</div>';
          el2.style.display='block';
          el2.innerHTML=ch;
          saveAccData();
        }).catch(function(){});
      })(orders[ci].id);
    }
  } catch(e){
    var el=document.getElementById('orderHistoryList');
    if(el)el.innerHTML='<div style="text-align:center;padding:30px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.3)">Ошибка загрузки</div>';
  }
}

// ===== FAVORITES =====
var FAVS=(function(){try{return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('fp_favs')||'[]')}catch(e){return []}})();
function saveFavs(){try{localStorage.setItem('fp_favs',JSON.stringify(FAVS))}catch(e){}}
function isFav(pid){return FAVS.indexOf(pid)>=0}
function heartSvg(){return '<svg viewBox="0 0 24 24"><defs><linearGradient id="favGrad" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="100%"><stop offset="0%" stop-color="#6e56ff"/><stop offset="100%" stop-color="#a855f7"/></linearGradient></defs><path d="M20.84 4.61a5.5 5.5 0 00-7.78 0L12 5.67l-1.06-1.06a5.5 5.5 0 00-7.78 7.78l1.06 1.06L12 21.23l7.78-7.78 1.06-1.06a5.5 5.5 0 000-7.78z"/></svg>'}
function toggleFav(pid,ev){
  if(ev)ev.stopPropagation();
  var idx=FAVS.indexOf(pid);
  var adding=idx<0;
  if(idx>=0){FAVS.splice(idx,1);}
  else{FAVS.push(pid);}
  saveFavs();
  var hearts=document.querySelectorAll('[data-fav="'+pid+'"]');
  hearts.forEach(function(h){h.classList.toggle('fav-on',isFav(pid))});
  var fb=document.getElementById('tabFavBadge');if(fb){fb.textContent=FAVS.length;fb.classList.toggle('z',FAVS.length===0)}
  if(currentTab==='fav')renderFavorites();
  // Server sync
  var tgUser=getTgUser();if(tgUser&&tgUser.id){
    apiFetch('/api/me/favorites',{method:adding?'POST':'DELETE',body:JSON.stringify({product_id:pid})}).catch(function(){});
  }
}
// Load favorites from server — сервер источник истины (чтобы удаления синхронизировались между устройствами)
function syncFavsFromServer(){
  // ZAHOD_Z_FAV_FIX guard убран — apiFetch шлёт cookie или Bearer, бэк решит
  apiFetch('/api/me/favorites').then(function(r){return r.json()}).then(function(d){
    if(!d||!Array.isArray(d.favorites))return;
    var server=(d.favorites||[]);
    /* V25_FAV_PURE_SERVER_TRUTH: убрана разовая миграция (V24) для симметрии с корзиной
       и устранения риска воскрешения на новом устройстве. Сервер БЕЗУСЛОВНО главный.
       Свежедобавленное не теряется — toggleFav() пушит на сервер сразу (POST), а
       syncFavsFromServer зовётся только на открытии/восстановлении сессии. */
    FAVS=server.slice();
    saveFavs();
    var fb=document.getElementById('tabFavBadge');if(fb){fb.textContent=FAVS.length;fb.classList.toggle('z',FAVS.length===0)}
    if(currentTab==='fav'&&typeof renderFavorites==='function'){try{renderFavorites()}catch(e){}} // ZAHOD_Z_FAV_FIX
  }).catch(function(){});
}
setTimeout(syncFavsFromServer,2000);

function renderFavorites(){
  var h='<div class="fav-header"><div class="fav-title">Избранное</div></div>';
  // Always visible info block
  h+='<div class="fav-info"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke="none" style="width:28px;height:28px;flex-shrink:0"><defs><linearGradient id="favGradInfo" x1="0%" y1="0%" x2="100%" y2="100%"><stop offset="0%" stop-color="#6e56ff"/><stop offset="100%" stop-color="#a855f7"/></linearGradient></defs><path fill="url(#favGradInfo)" d="M20.84 4.61a5.5 5.5 0 00-7.78 0L12 5.67l-1.06-1.06a5.5 5.5 0 00-7.78 7.78l1.06 1.06L12 21.23l7.78-7.78 1.06-1.06a5.5 5.5 0 000-7.78z"/></svg><span>Бот уведомит вас, если товар из Избранного начнёт продаваться со скидкой.</span></div>';
  if(!FAVS.length){
    h+='<div class="fav-empty"><div class="fav-empty-t">Пока нет избранных товаров</div></div>';
  } else {
    h+='<div class="fav-list">';
    for(var i=0;i<FAVS.length;i++){
      var p=D?D.products[FAVS[i]]:null;
      if(!p)continue;
      var pr=gP(p);var cp=pr.price;var co=pr.oldPrice;
      var disc=co&&cp?dc(co,cp):0;
      var _favDeal=getSubDeal(p);var _favHasPsp=!!_favDeal;var _favPsp=_favDeal?_favDeal.price:null;var _favKind=_favDeal?_favDeal.kind:'ps';
      var _favDisplayPrice=_favHasPsp?_favPsp:cp;
      var _favDisc=disc;
      if(!_favDisc&&_favHasPsp)_favDisc=dc(cp,_favPsp);
      h+='<div class="fav-item" onclick="oM(\''+es(FAVS[i])+'\')">';
      h+='<img class="fav-item-img" src="'+_thumb(p.photo,160)+'" onerror="this.style.display=\'none\'">';
      h+='<div class="fav-item-info">';
      var _favSubBadge='';
      if(!disc&&_favHasPsp){
        if(_favKind==='ea')_favSubBadge=' <span class="fav-item-disc" style="color:#ff4444;background:rgba(255,68,68,.15);display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:2px">'+eaPlayImg(12)+' -'+_favDisc+'%</span>';
        else _favSubBadge=' <span class="fav-item-disc" style="color:#f5a623;background:rgba(245,166,35,.15);display:inline-flex;align-items:center;gap:2px">'+psPlusSvg(12)+' -'+_favDisc+'%</span>';
      }
      h+='<div class="fav-item-price">'+(_favDisplayPrice?fm(_favDisplayPrice):'')+(disc?' <span class="fav-item-disc">-'+disc+'%</span>':'')+_favSubBadge+'</div>';
      h+='<div class="fav-item-name">'+es(p.name)+'</div>';
      var _favDiscEnd=getDiscountEnd(p);
      if(_favDiscEnd&&((co&&cp)||_favHasPsp)){var _favRem=_favDiscEnd-Date.now();if(_favRem>0){h+='<div class="fav-item-detail" data-disc-end="'+_favDiscEnd+'"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5" style="width:11px;height:11px;flex-shrink:0;opacity:.5"><circle cx="12" cy="13" r="8"/><path d="M12 9v4l2 2"/><path d="M9 2h6"/></svg> Скидка ещё '+fmtCountdown(_favRem)+'</div>';}}
      h+='</div>';
      h+='<button class="fav-item-del" onclick="event.stopPropagation();toggleFav(\''+es(FAVS[i])+'\')"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" style="width:20px;height:20px"><path d="M3 6h18M8 6V4a2 2 0 012-2h4a2 2 0 012 2v2m3 0v14a2 2 0 01-2 2H7a2 2 0 01-2-2V6h14"/></svg></button>';
      h+='</div>';
    }
    h+='</div>';
  }
  h+='<div style="height:80px"></div>';
  document.getElementById('favPage').innerHTML=h;
}

// ===== CATALOG PAGE (Services/AI/etc) =====
function renderCatalogPage(){
  
  _catSubSection=null;_catSubSearch='';_catSubSearchOpen=false;
  if(_cameFromWelcome){tgBack(true,function(){_backToWelcome();});}else{tgBack(true,function(){switchTab('home');});}
  document.getElementById('catPage').classList.add('catsub-bg');
  var h='<div class="cat-content" style="padding-top:12px">';

  // AI Banner — compact, top of catalog
  h+='<div class="cat-ai-banner" onclick="openAiChat()">';
  h+='<div class="cat-ai-banner-icon"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor"><path d="M9.937 15.5A2 2 0 0 0 8.5 14.063l-6.135-1.582a.5.5 0 0 1 0-.962L8.5 9.936A2 2 0 0 0 9.937 8.5l1.582-6.135a.5.5 0 0 1 .963 0L14.063 8.5A2 2 0 0 0 15.5 9.937l6.135 1.581a.5.5 0 0 1 0 .964L15.5 14.063a2 2 0 0 0-1.437 1.437l-1.582 6.135a.5.5 0 0 1-.963 0z"/><path d="M20 3v4M22 5h-4"/></svg></div>';
  h+='<div class="cat-ai-banner-text"><div class="cat-ai-banner-title">Не знаешь что выбрать? <span>Спроси ИИ</span></div><div class="cat-ai-banner-sub">Подберём игру, нейросеть или сервис</div></div>';
  h+='<div class="cat-ai-banner-arrow"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><path d="M9 18l6-6-6-6"/></svg></div>';
  h+='</div>';

  // Render catalog carousels from collections with target=catalog or both
  if(D&&D.collections){
    var catCols=D.collections.filter(function(c){return c.target==='catalog'||c.target==='both'}).sort(function(a,b){return a.position-b.position});
    for(var ci=0;ci<catCols.length;ci++){
      var c=catCols[ci];
      var ps=[];for(var j=0;j<c.items.length;j++){var p=D.products[c.items[j]];if(p&&(p.type==='nav_card'||p.type==='donate'||p.type==='service'||p.type==='ai'||p.type==='key'||(R==='TR'?p.price_tr:p.price)))ps.push(p);}
      if(!ps.length)continue;
      // Detect if this collection maps to a catalogCategories section
      var _catSection=_detectCatSection(c);
      h+='<section class="se"><div class="seh"><h2 class="set">'+es(c.title)+'</h2>';
      h+='<div class="ar">';
      h+='<button class="abtn" data-c="cc_'+c.id+'" onclick="sC(this.dataset.c,-1)">\u2039</button>';
      h+='<button class="abtn" data-c="cc_'+c.id+'" onclick="sC(this.dataset.c,1)">\u203A</button>'; /* ZAHOD_N_CAT_ARROWS */
      if(_catSection){
        h+='<button class="cat-show-all" onclick="showCatSubcategories(\''+_catSection+'\')">Показать все <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><path d="M9 18l6-6-6-6"/></svg></button>';
      } else {
        h+='<button class="cat-show-all" onclick="showCatCollection('+c.id+')">Показать все <svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><path d="M9 18l6-6-6-6"/></svg></button>';
      }
      h+='</div></div>';
      h+='<div class="ca" id="cc_'+c.id+'">';
      for(var j=0;j<ps.length;j++)h+=cH(ps[j],false);
      h+='</div></section>';
    }
  }

  h+='</div>'; // close cat-content

  // Fallback categories if no catalog collections yet
  if(!D||!D.collections||!D.collections.filter(function(c){return c.target==='catalog'||c.target==='both'}).length){
    var counts={game:0,preorder:0,service:0,ai:0,key:0,donate:0};
    if(D&&D.products){var all=Object.values(D.products);for(var i=0;i<all.length;i++){if(counts[all[i].type]!==undefined)counts[all[i].type]++;}}
    h+='<div class="cat-grid">';
    h+='<div class="cat-card" onclick="switchTab(\'home\')"><div class="cat-card-icon">🎮</div><div class="cat-card-name">Игры</div><div class="cat-card-cnt">'+(counts.game+counts.preorder)+' товаров</div></div>';
    h+='<div class="cat-card" onclick="showCatSubcategories(\'service\')"><div class="cat-card-icon">🛠</div><div class="cat-card-name">Сервисы</div><div class="cat-card-cnt">'+counts.service+' товаров</div></div>';
    h+='<div class="cat-card" onclick="showCatSubcategories(\'ai\')"><div class="cat-card-icon">🤖</div><div class="cat-card-name">Нейросети</div><div class="cat-card-cnt">'+counts.ai+' товаров</div></div>';
    h+='<div class="cat-card" onclick="showCatSection(\'key\')"><div class="cat-card-icon">🔑</div><div class="cat-card-name">Ключи и коды</div><div class="cat-card-cnt">'+counts.key+' товаров</div></div>';
    h+='<div class="cat-card" onclick="showCatSection(\'donate\')"><div class="cat-card-icon">💎</div><div class="cat-card-name">Донат</div><div class="cat-card-cnt">'+counts.donate+' товаров</div></div>';
    h+='<div class="cat-card" onclick="sD(\'nav_playstation_store\')"><div class="cat-card-icon">🕹</div><div class="cat-card-name">PS Store</div></div>';
    h+='<div class="cat-card" onclick="openSteam()"><div class="cat-card-icon">🎯</div><div class="cat-card-name">Steam</div></div>';
    h+='</div>';
  }

  h+='<div style="height:100px"></div>';
  document.getElementById('catPage').innerHTML=h;
}

function openAiChat(){
  _aiPrevBackFn=_tgBackFn;
  // Cancel any pending close animation
  if(_aiCloseTimer){clearTimeout(_aiCloseTimer);_aiCloseTimer=null;}
  _aiClosing=false;
  var overlay=document.getElementById('aiOverlay');
  var chat=document.getElementById('aiChat');
  // Force clean state
  chat.style.visibility='';
  chat.classList.remove('no-transition');
  overlay.style.display='block';
  chat.style.display='flex';
  chat.classList.add('visible');
  chat.offsetHeight;
  overlay.classList.add('open');
  chat.classList.add('open');
  document.body.style.overflow='hidden';
  tgBack(true,function(){closeAiChat();});
  if(!document.getElementById('aiMsgs').children.length){
    _aiHistory=[];
    _aiShownProducts=[];
    _aiLastIntents=null;
    _renderAiQuick();
    _addAiMsg('bot','Йоу! Я твой бро по играм, нейросетям и подпискам. Скидывай что ищешь — подберу топчик 🎮');
  }
  if(!_aiResizeSet){
    _aiResizeSet=true;
    if(window.visualViewport){
      window.visualViewport.addEventListener('resize',_aiViewportResize);
      window.visualViewport.addEventListener('scroll',_aiViewportResize);
    }
  }
}
var _aiResizeSet=false;
var _aiKbdHeight=0;
var _aiKbdPoll=0;
var _aiBlurTime=0;
function _aiViewportResize(){
  var chat=document.getElementById('aiChat');
  if(!chat||!chat.classList.contains('open'))return;
  // After blur, ignore resize events for 1.5s to prevent overwriting reset
  if(_aiBlurTime && Date.now()-_aiBlurTime<1500)return;
  var vv=window.visualViewport;
  if(vv){
    var kbdOpen=vv.height < window.innerHeight - 50;
    if(kbdOpen){
      chat.style.height=vv.height+'px';
      chat.style.top=vv.offsetTop+'px';
    } else {
      chat.style.height='';
      chat.style.top='';
    }
  }
  var msgs=document.getElementById('aiMsgs');
  msgs.scrollTop=msgs.scrollHeight;
}
function _aiStartPoll(){
  _aiStopPoll();
  _aiKbdPoll=setInterval(function(){
    var vv=window.visualViewport;
    if(!vv)return;
    var chat=document.getElementById('aiChat');
    if(!chat||!chat.classList.contains('open')){_aiStopPoll();return;}
    var kbdOpen=vv.height < window.innerHeight - 50;
    if(!kbdOpen&&chat.style.height){
      chat.style.height='';
      chat.style.top='';
    }
  },100);
}
function _aiStopPoll(){
  if(_aiKbdPoll){clearInterval(_aiKbdPoll);_aiKbdPoll=0;}
}

function closeAiChat(){
  _aiWasOpen=false;
  _aiClosing=true;
  _aiStopPoll();
  if(_aiCloseTimer){clearTimeout(_aiCloseTimer);_aiCloseTimer=null;}
  var inp=document.getElementById('aiInput');if(inp)inp.blur();
  var overlay=document.getElementById('aiOverlay');
  var chat=document.getElementById('aiChat');
  // Restore previous back button handler
  if(_aiPrevBackFn){tgBack(true,_aiPrevBackFn);}else if(_cameFromWelcome){tgBack(true,function(){_backToWelcome()});}else{tgBack(false);}
  _aiPrevBackFn=null;
  // Start slide-down immediately (keep current height so no jump)
  overlay.classList.remove('open');
  chat.classList.remove('open');
  _aiCloseTimer=setTimeout(function(){
    _aiCloseTimer=null;
    _aiClosing=false;
    overlay.style.display='none';
    chat.style.display='none';
    chat.classList.remove('visible');
    chat.style.visibility='';
    chat.style.height='';chat.style.top='';
    document.body.style.overflow='';
  },600);
}

function _renderAiQuick(){
  var h='';
  for(var i=0;i<AI_QUICK_BTNS.length;i++){
    h+='<button class="ai-quick-btn" onclick="sendAiQuick('+i+')">'+AI_QUICK_BTNS[i].text+'</button>';
  }
  document.getElementById('aiQuick').innerHTML=h;
}

function sendAiQuick(idx){
  document.getElementById('aiQuick').innerHTML='';
  var btn=(_aiContextBtns&&_aiContextBtns[idx])?_aiContextBtns[idx]:AI_QUICK_BTNS[idx];
  if(!btn)return;
  // "Пополнить Steam" button -> navigate to Steam page
  if(btn.text&&btn.text.toLowerCase().indexOf('steam')>=0&&btn.text.toLowerCase().indexOf('пополн')>=0){
    closeAiChat();
    setTimeout(function(){openSteam();},400);
    return;
  }
  sendAiMsg(btn.msg);
}

var _aiContextBtns=null;
var _aiShownProducts = []; // Track all shown product IDs for dedup
var _aiLastIntents = null; // Track last response intents for "Показать ещё" context
function _showContextBtns(userMsg, products, botText, serverButtons){
  var btns=[];

  // Use buttons from Claude if provided
  if(serverButtons&&serverButtons.length){
    for(var i=0;i<serverButtons.length;i++){
      btns.push({text:serverButtons[i],msg:serverButtons[i]});
    }
  } else if(!products||!products.length){
    // No products and no buttons — show defaults
    btns.push({text:'Подобрать игру',msg:'Подбери мне игру на PlayStation'});
    btns.push({text:'Нейросети',msg:'Какую нейросеть посоветуешь?'});
    btns.push({text:'Топ скидки',msg:'Что сейчас с самыми большими скидками?'});
    btns.push({text:'Новинки',msg:'Покажи новинки'});
  } else {
    // Products but no buttons from server — generic fallback
    btns.push({text:'Показать ещё',msg:'Покажи ещё варианты, другие'});
    btns.push({text:'Подешевле',msg:'Есть варианты подешевле?'});
    btns.push({text:'Что популярно',msg:'Что сейчас самое популярное?'});
  }

  _aiContextBtns=btns;
  var h='';
  for(var i=0;i<btns.length;i++){
    h+='<button class="ai-quick-btn" onclick="sendAiQuick('+i+')">'+btns[i].text+'</button>';
  }
  document.getElementById('aiQuick').innerHTML=h;
}

function _addAiMsg(role, text, products){
  var msgs=document.getElementById('aiMsgs');
  var div=document.createElement('div');
  div.className='ai-msg '+(role==='user'?'user':'bot');
  var html=es(text).replace(/\n/g,'<br>');
  if(products&&products.length&&D&&D.products){
    html+='<div class="ai-msg-products">';
    for(var i=0;i<products.length;i++){
      var p=D.products[products[i]];
      if(!p)continue;
      var price=R==='TR'?p.price_tr:p.price;
      html+='<div class="ai-prod-card" onclick="_aiOpenProduct(\''+es(p.id)+'\')">';
      html+='<img src="'+_thumb(p.photo,300)+'" onerror="this.style.display=\'none\'" loading="lazy">';
      html+='<div class="ai-prod-name">'+es(p.name)+'</div>';
      if(price)html+='<div class="ai-prod-price">'+price+' ₽</div>';
      html+='</div>';
    }
    html+='</div>';
  }
  div.innerHTML=html;
  msgs.appendChild(div);
  msgs.scrollTop=msgs.scrollHeight;
}

function _aiReturnToChat(){
  
  _aiWasOpen=false;
  if(_aiCloseTimer){clearTimeout(_aiCloseTimer);_aiCloseTimer=null;}
  var chat=document.getElementById('aiChat');
  var overlay=document.getElementById('aiOverlay');
  chat.style.visibility='';
  chat.style.display='flex';
  chat.classList.add('visible','open');
  overlay.style.display='block';
  overlay.classList.add('open');
  document.body.style.overflow='hidden';
  var msgs=document.getElementById('aiMsgs');
  msgs.scrollTop=msgs.scrollHeight;
  if(window.visualViewport)_aiViewportResize();
  tgBack(true,function(){closeAiChat();});
}

function _aiOpenProduct(id){
  
  // Mark that AI chat is open so cM() knows to return here
  _aiWasOpen=true;
  var chat=document.getElementById('aiChat');
  var overlay=document.getElementById('aiOverlay');
  chat.style.visibility='hidden';
  overlay.style.display='none';
  overlay.classList.remove('open');
  document.body.style.overflow='';
  oM(id);
  
}

function _showAiTyping(){
  var msgs=document.getElementById('aiMsgs');
  var div=document.createElement('div');
  div.className='ai-typing';div.id='aiTyping';
  div.innerHTML='<span></span><span></span><span></span>';
  msgs.appendChild(div);
  msgs.scrollTop=msgs.scrollHeight;
}
function _hideAiTyping(){var t=document.getElementById('aiTyping');if(t)t.remove();}

async function sendAiMsg(text){
  if(_aiSending)return;
  var inp=document.getElementById('aiInput');
  var msg=text||inp.value.trim();
  if(!msg)return;
  inp.value='';
  document.getElementById('aiQuick').innerHTML='';
  _aiContextBtns=null;
  _addAiMsg('user',msg);
  _aiHistory.push({role:'user',content:msg});
  _aiSending=true;
  document.getElementById('aiSend').disabled=true;
  _showAiTyping();
  try{
    var tgUser=getTgUser();
    var body={message:msg,region:R,telegram_id:tgUser?tgUser.id:null,history:_aiHistory.slice(-6),shown_product_ids:_aiShownProducts.slice()};
    // text param means button click — pass context for continuity; manual input — reset context
    if(text&&_aiLastIntents&&_aiLastIntents.length){body.context={intents:_aiLastIntents};}
    if(!text){_aiLastIntents=null;}
    var r=await apiFetch('/api/ai/ask',{method:'POST',body:JSON.stringify(body)}); // ZAHOD_Z_FINAL_AI
    var d=await r.json();
    // Track shown products for dedup
    if(d.products&&d.products.length){
      for(var pi=0;pi<d.products.length;pi++){
        if(_aiShownProducts.indexOf(d.products[pi])<0)_aiShownProducts.push(d.products[pi]);
      }
    }
    // Save intents for "Показать ещё" context continuity
    if(d.intents&&d.intents.length){_aiLastIntents=d.intents;}
    _hideAiTyping();
    if(d.error){_addAiMsg('bot',d.error);} 
    else{
      _addAiMsg('bot',d.text||'Не удалось получить ответ',d.products||[]);
      if(d.text)_aiHistory.push({role:'assistant',content:d.text});
      // Show context buttons after response
      _showContextBtns(msg, d.products||[], d.text||'', d.buttons||[]);
    }
  }catch(e){_hideAiTyping();_addAiMsg('bot','Ошибка сети. Попробуй ещё раз.');}
  _aiSending=false;
  document.getElementById('aiSend').disabled=false;
}

// Detect if a collection title maps to ai or service section
function _detectCatSection(col){
  if(!D||!D.catalogCategories)return null;
  var tl=col.title.toLowerCase();
  if((tl.indexOf('нейросет')>=0||tl.indexOf('ai')>=0||tl.indexOf('ии')>=0)&&D.catalogCategories.ai&&D.catalogCategories.ai.length)return 'ai';
  if((tl.indexOf('сервис')>=0||tl.indexOf('service')>=0)&&D.catalogCategories.service&&D.catalogCategories.service.length)return 'service';
  return null;
}

// ===== SUBCATEGORY PAGE (AI / Services) =====
var _catSubGridMode=false; // false=carousel, true=grid
var _catSubSection=null; // current section
var _catSubSearch=''; // search query

function showCatSubcategories(section, _restore){
  _catSubSection=section;
  if(!_restore){_catSubGridMode=false;_catSubSearch='';_catSubSearchOpen=false;}
  tgBack(true,function(){renderCatalogPage();});
  _renderCatSub();
  document.getElementById('catPage').classList.add('catsub-bg');
  if(!_restore)document.getElementById('catPage').scrollTop=0;
}

function _renderCatSub(){
  var section=_catSubSection;
  if(!D||!D.catalogCategories||!D.catalogCategories[section])return;
  var cats=D.catalogCategories[section];
  var titles={ai:'Нейросети',service:'Сервисы'};
  var q=_normSearch(_catSubSearch);

  // Toggle button
  var h='<div class="catsub-toggle-row">';
  h+='<div class="catsub-toggle-btn'+(_catSubGridMode?' active':'')+'" onclick="_toggleCatSubView()">';
  if(_catSubGridMode){
    h+='<svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><rect x="3" y="3" width="7" height="7" rx="1"/><rect x="14" y="3" width="7" height="7" rx="1"/><rect x="3" y="14" width="7" height="7" rx="1"/><rect x="14" y="14" width="7" height="7" rx="1"/></svg>';
  } else {
    h+='<svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><rect x="3" y="3" width="18" height="7" rx="1"/><rect x="3" y="14" width="18" height="7" rx="1"/></svg>';
  }
  h+='</div></div>';
  // Content with same padding as main .mn
  h+='<div class="catsub-content" style="padding:0 16px 100px">';

  var totalShown=0;
  for(var ci=0;ci<cats.length;ci++){
    var cat=cats[ci];
    var ps=[];
    if(cat.items&&cat.items.length){
      for(var j=0;j<cat.items.length;j++){
        var p=D.products[cat.items[j]];
        if(!p)continue;
        if(_catSubGridMode&&p.type==='nav_card')continue;
        if(q){if(!p._nameNorm)p._nameNorm=_normSearch(p.name);if(p._nameNorm.indexOf(q)<0)continue;}
        if(p.type!=='nav_card'&&p.type!=='service'&&p.type!=='ai'&&p.type!=='donate'&&p.type!=='key'){
          if(!(R==='TR'?p.price_tr:p.price))continue;
        }
        ps.push(p);
      }
    }
    if(!ps.length)continue;
    
    // Use same .se/.set/.ca classes as main page
    h+='<section class="se">';
    var _subCaId='csub_'+cat.id; /* ZAHOD_N_CAT_ARROWS */
    h+='<div class="seh"><h2 class="set">'+(cat.icon?cat.icon+' ':'')+es(cat.title)+'</h2>';
    if(!_catSubGridMode){h+='<div class="ar"><button class="abtn" data-c="'+_subCaId+'" onclick="sC(this.dataset.c,-1)">\u2039</button><button class="abtn" data-c="'+_subCaId+'" onclick="sC(this.dataset.c,1)">\u203A</button></div>';}
    h+='</div>';
    
    if(_catSubGridMode){
      h+='<div class="gr catsub-anim-in">';
      for(var j=0;j<ps.length;j++)h+=cH(ps[j],true);
      h+='</div>';
    } else {
      h+='<div class="ca catsub-anim-in" id="'+_subCaId+'">';
      for(var j=0;j<ps.length;j++)h+=cH(ps[j],false);
      h+='</div>';
    }
    h+='</section>';
    totalShown+=ps.length;
  }

  if(q&&totalShown===0){
    h+='<div class="catsub-empty">Ничего не найдено</div>';
  }

  h+='</div>';
  document.getElementById('catPage').innerHTML=h;
}

var _catSubSearchTimer=null;

function _catSubSearchInput(v){
  _catSubSearch=v;
  if(_catSubSearchTimer)clearTimeout(_catSubSearchTimer);
  _catSubSearchTimer=setTimeout(function(){_renderCatSub();},250);
}

function _toggleCatSubView(){
  // Animate out all cards (scoped to catPage only!)
  var cp=document.getElementById('catPage');
  var containers=cp.querySelectorAll('.ca, .gr');
  for(var i=0;i<containers.length;i++)containers[i].classList.add('catsub-anim-out');
  setTimeout(function(){
    _catSubGridMode=!_catSubGridMode;
    _renderCatSub();
  },300);
}

function showCatCollection(cid){
  if(!D||!D.collections)return;
  var col=null;for(var i=0;i<D.collections.length;i++){if(D.collections[i].id===cid||D.collections[i].id===parseInt(cid)){col=D.collections[i];break;}}
  if(!col)return;
  // Check if this collection has a catalogCategories mapping
  var _cs=_detectCatSection(col);
  if(_cs){showCatSubcategories(_cs);return;}
  var ps=[];for(var j=0;j<col.items.length;j++){var p=D.products[col.items[j]];if(p&&(p.type==='nav_card'||p.type==='donate'||p.type==='service'||p.type==='ai'||p.type==='key'||(R==='TR'?p.price_tr:p.price)))ps.push(p);}
  if(!ps.length)return;
  var h='<div style="padding:0 16px">';
  h+='<div class="cat-sec-back" onclick="renderCatalogPage()"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><path d="M15 18l-6-6 6-6"/></svg>Каталог</div>';
  h+='<div class="cat-sec-title">'+es(col.title)+'</div>';
  h+='<div class="cat-sec-grid">';
  for(var j=0;j<ps.length;j++)h+=cH(ps[j],true);
  h+='</div></div><div style="height:100px"></div>';
  document.getElementById('catPage').innerHTML=h;
  document.getElementById('catPage').scrollTop=0;
}
function showCatSection(type){
  // For ai/service with catalogCategories, redirect to subcategories
  if((type==='ai'||type==='service')&&D&&D.catalogCategories&&D.catalogCategories[type]&&D.catalogCategories[type].length){
    showCatSubcategories(type);return;
  }
  if(!D)return;
  var items=[];var all=Object.values(D.products);
  for(var i=0;i<all.length;i++){if(all[i].type===type)items.push(all[i])}
  var titles={service:'Сервисы',ai:'Нейросети',key:'Ключи и коды',donate:'Донат'};
  var h='<div style="padding:0 16px">';
  h+='<div class="cat-sec-back" onclick="renderCatalogPage()"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2.5"><path d="M15 18l-6-6 6-6"/></svg>Каталог</div>';
  h+='<div class="cat-sec-title">'+titles[type]+' <span style="font-size:14px;color:rgba(255,255,255,.35);font-weight:600">'+items.length+'</span></div>';
  h+='<div class="cat-sec-grid">';
  for(var i=0;i<items.length;i++)h+=cH(items[i],true);
  h+='</div></div><div style="height:100px"></div>';
  document.getElementById('catPage').innerHTML=h;
  document.getElementById('catPage').scrollTop=0;
}

// Tab bar auto-hide + header .sc on catalog page scroll
(function(){
  var _catLastSY=0;
  // Attach directly to catPage instead of document capture (avoids intercepting all scroll events)
  var cp=document.getElementById('catPage');
  if(cp){
    cp.addEventListener('scroll',function(){
      if(!cp.classList.contains('show'))return;
      var sy=cp.scrollTop;var delta=sy-_catLastSY;
      var bar=document.getElementById('tabBar');
      if(bar){
        if(delta>8&&sy>60)bar.classList.add('hidden');
        else if(delta<-5)bar.classList.remove('hidden');
      }
      var hd=document.getElementById('hd');
      if(hd)hd.classList.toggle('sc',sy>30);
      _catLastSY=sy;
    },{passive:true});
  }
})();

// ===== CART TAB =====
function renderCartTab(){
  var _savedPromo=_tabPromoData;
  _tabPromoData=null;
  var validCart=[];for(var i=0;i<CART.length;i++){if(getCartItemInfo(CART[i]))validCart.push(CART[i]);}
  if(validCart.length!==CART.length){CART=validCart;saveCart();}
  var total=0;
  for(var i=0;i<CART.length;i++){var info=getCartItemInfo(CART[i]);if(info)total+=Number(info.price)||0;}
  // Restore promo if cart still has items
  if(CART.length&&_savedPromo)_tabPromoData=_savedPromo;

  if(!CART.length){
    var h='<div style="padding:20px"><div class="cart-ttl" style="font-size:28px;font-weight:900">Корзина</div></div>';
    h+='<div class="cart-body" style="padding:0 20px">';
    h+='<div class="cart-empty"><svg viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5"><path d="M6 2L3 6v14a2 2 0 002 2h14a2 2 0 002-2V6l-3-4z"/><line x1="3" y1="6" x2="21" y2="6"/><path d="M16 10a4 4 0 01-8 0"/></svg><div class="cart-empty-t">Корзина пуста</div><div class="cart-empty-s">Добавьте товары из каталога</div></div>';
    h+='</div>';
    document.getElementById('cartPage').innerHTML=h;
    tgBack(true,function(){_closeCartToOrigin()});
    return;
  }

  orderStep='form';
  var cats=getCartCategories();

  // Header
  var h='<div style="padding:20px 20px 0"><div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:baseline"><div class="cart-ttl" style="font-size:28px;font-weight:900">Корзина</div><div id="cartHeaderPrice" style="font-size:28px;font-weight:900;color:#a78bfa;text-align:right">'+fm(total)+'</div></div></div>';
  h+='<div class="cart-body" style="padding:0 20px">';

  // Cart items
  h+='<div class="chk-section">';
  var grouped=[];var keyGroups={};
  for(var i=0;i<CART.length;i++){
    var ci=CART[i];var p=D?D.products[ci.pid]:null;
    if(p&&p.type==='key'){
      if(!keyGroups[ci.pid]){keyGroups[ci.pid]={ci:ci,count:0,unitPrice:Number(ci.price)||Number(p.price_tr)||Number(p.price)||0};grouped.push({type:'key',pid:ci.pid});}
      keyGroups[ci.pid].count++;
    } else {grouped.push({type:'item',ci:ci});}
  }
  for(var g=0;g<grouped.length;g++){
    if(grouped[g].type==='key'){
      var kg=keyGroups[grouped[g].pid];if(!kg)continue;
      var info=getCartItemInfo(kg.ci);if(!info)continue;
      var lt=kg.unitPrice*kg.count;
      h+='<div class="chk-item" style="position:relative">';
      h+='<img class="chk-item-img" src="'+es(info.photo)+'" onerror="this.style.opacity=\'0.3\'">';
      h+='<div class="chk-item-info"><div class="chk-item-name">'+es(info.name)+'</div>';
      if(info.meta)h+='<div class="chk-item-meta">'+es(info.meta)+'</div>';
      h+='<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;margin-top:6px">';
      h+='<button style="width:28px;height:28px;border-radius:8px;border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.12);background:rgba(255,255,255,.06);color:#fff;font-size:16px;cursor:pointer;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center" onclick="cartTabKeyQty(\''+es(grouped[g].pid)+'\',-1)">\u2212</button>';
      h+='<span style="font-size:14px;font-weight:700;min-width:20px;text-align:center">'+kg.count+'</span>';
      h+='<button style="width:28px;height:28px;border-radius:8px;border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.12);background:rgba(255,255,255,.06);color:#fff;font-size:16px;cursor:pointer;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center" onclick="cartTabKeyQty(\''+es(grouped[g].pid)+'\',1)">+</button>';
      h+='<span style="color:#888;font-size:12px">\u00d7 '+fm(kg.unitPrice)+'</span></div>';
      h+='<div style="margin-top:4px"><span class="chk-item-price">'+fm(lt)+'</span></div>';
      h+='</div>';
      h+='<button onclick="removeAllKeys(\''+es(grouped[g].pid)+'\');renderCartTab()" style="flex-shrink:0;width:36px;height:36px;border-radius:10px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.06);border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.1);color:rgba(255,255,255,.4);cursor:pointer;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M3 6h18M8 6V4a2 2 0 012-2h4a2 2 0 012 2v2m3 0v14a2 2 0 01-2 2H7a2 2 0 01-2-2V6h14"/></svg></button>';
      h+='</div>';
    } else {
      var ci=grouped[g].ci;var info=getCartItemInfo(ci);if(!info)continue;
      h+='<div class="chk-item" style="position:relative">';
      h+='<img class="chk-item-img" src="'+es(info.photo)+'" onerror="this.style.opacity=\'0.3\'">';
      h+='<div class="chk-item-info"><div class="chk-item-name">'+es(info.name)+'</div>';
      h+='<div style="margin-top:4px;display:flex;align-items:center;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:4px">';
      if(info.oldPrice){h+='<span style="font-size:14px;font-weight:700;color:#ff3b5c">'+fm(info.price)+'</span><span style="font-size:12px;color:#666;text-decoration:line-through">'+fm(info.oldPrice)+'</span>';}
      else{h+='<span style="font-size:14px;font-weight:700">'+fm(info.price)+'</span>';}
      if(info.meta)h+='<span style="font-size:12px;color:#888"> \u2022 '+es(info.meta)+'</span>';
      h+='</div></div>';
      h+='<button onclick="removeFromCart(\''+es(ci.key.replace(/'/g,"\\\\\'"))+'\');renderCartTab()" style="flex-shrink:0;width:36px;height:36px;border-radius:10px;background:rgba(255,255,255,.06);border:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,.1);color:rgba(255,255,255,.4);cursor:pointer;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center"><svg width="16" height="16" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2"><path d="M3 6h18M8 6V4a2 2 0 012-2h4a2 2 0 012 2v2m3 0v14a2 2 0 01-2 2H7a2 2 0 01-2-2V6h14"/></svg></button>';
      h+='</div>';
    }
  }
  h+='</div>';

  // PS section
  if(cats.ps){
    h+='<div class="chk-section"><div class="chk-label">Куда оформить заказ?</div>';
    h+='<div class="chk-toggle"><button class="chk-tog-btn'+(accMode==='own'?' on':'')+'" onclick="accMode=\'own\';renderCartTab()">На мой аккаунт</button>';
    h+='<button class="chk-tog-btn'+(accMode==='create'?' on':'')+'" onclick="accMode=\'create\';renderCartTab()">Создайте аккаунт</button></div>';
    if(accMode==='own'){
      var rKey=R.toLowerCase();
      var savedLogin=ACC_DATA['psLogin_'+rKey]||'';
      var savedPass=ACC_DATA['psPass_'+rKey]||'';
      var codes=ACC_DATA['backupCodes_'+rKey]||[];
      var availCode='';var availCodeIdx=-1;for(var ci2=0;ci2<codes.length;ci2++){if(!codes[ci2].used){availCode=codes[ci2].code;availCodeIdx=ci2;break;}}
      h+='<div class="chk-hint">Укажите данные вашего PlayStation аккаунта ('+(R==='UA'?'Украина':'Турция')+')</div>';
      h+='<input class="cart-input" id="psLogin" placeholder="Логин (почта PSN)" value="'+es(savedLogin)+'" oninput="var _r=R.toLowerCase();ACC_DATA[\'psLogin_\'+_r]=this.value;saveAccData([\'ps_account_\'+_r])">';
      h+='<div style="position:relative"><input class="cart-input" id="psPass" type="password" placeholder="Пароль" value="'+es(savedPass)+'" style="padding-right:44px" oninput="var _r=R.toLowerCase();ACC_DATA[\'psPass_\'+_r]=this.value;saveAccData([\'ps_account_\'+_r])"><button onclick="_togglePassVis(this)" type="button" style="position:absolute;right:12px;top:50%;transform:translateY(-50%);background:none;border:none;padding:4px;cursor:pointer;display:flex;align-items:center"><svg width="18" height="18" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="none" stroke="rgba(255,255,255,.2)" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"><path d="M17.94 17.94A10.07 10.07 0 0 1 12 20c-7 0-11-8-11-8a18.45 18.45 0 0 1 5.06-5.94M9.9 4.24A9.12 9.12 0 0 1 12 4c7 0 11 8 11 8a18.5 18.5 0 0 1-2.16 3.19m-6.72-1.07a3 3 0 1 1-4.24-4.24"/><line x1="1" y1="1" x2="23" y2="23"/></svg></button></div>';
      h+='<input class="cart-input" id="psCode" placeholder="Резервный код 2FA (если включена)" value="'+es(availCode)+'" style="margin-bottom:0">';
      if(availCode){h+='<div style="font-size:11px;color:rgba(110,86,255,.7);margin-top:8px;margin-bottom:-6px">Код подставлен из сохранённых (осталось: '+(codes.filter(function(c){return!c.used}).length-1)+')</div>';}
    } else {
      h+='<div class="chk-hint">Мы бесплатно создадим аккаунт, оформим покупку и передадим вам все данные для доступа</div>';
      // PS Plus upsell — reuse standard .sc subscription cards
      var _hasPsSub=false;for(var _si2=0;_si2<CART.length;_si2++){if(CART[_si2].sub&&CART[_si2].subGroup==='ps'){_hasPsSub=true;break;}}
      if(!_hasPsSub){
        var _uPeriod=P.pp||12;var _uPl=_uPeriod===1?'1 месяц':_uPeriod===3?'3 месяца':'12 месяцев';var _uRl=R==='UA'?'Украина':'Турция';
        h+='<div style="margin-top:10px"><div class="chk-label">Добавим подписку?</div>';
        h+='<div class="chk-hint" style="margin-bottom:6px">Для онлайн-игры нужна подписка PS\u00a0Plus</div>';
        h+='<div class="sg">';
        for(var _ui=0;_ui<SB.ps.tiers.length;_ui++){
          var _ut=SB.ps.tiers[_ui];var _up=_ut.p[R][_uPeriod];
          h+='<div class="sc" data-upsell-tier="'+es(_ut.n)+'">';
          if(SI&&SI[_ut.ik])h+='<img class="sci" src="'+SI[_ut.ik]+'">';
